# <a name="required-mobile-diagnostic-data-for-microsoft-teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="35c5f-103">Microsoft Teams의 필수 모바일 진단 데이터</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-103">Required mobile diagnostic data for Microsoft Teams</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="35c5f-104">다음 문서는 Microsoft Teams 모바일 이벤트 목록과 각 이벤트에서 수집하는 속성 목록을 포함합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-104">The following article contains a list of Microsoft Teams mobile events, and lists of properties each event collects.</span></span>

## <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="35c5f-105">이벤트</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-105">Events</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-106">아래에 나열된 모든 이벤트에 대한 공통 속성이 있습니다. 이를 검토하려면 [모든 이벤트와 함께 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-all-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-106">There are common properties for all events listed below, to review them, see [Properties sent with all events](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span></span>

### <a name="panelaction"></a><span data-ttu-id="35c5f-107">PanelAction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-107">PanelAction</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-108">PanelAction 이벤트의 속성에 대한 자세한 내용은 [panelaction 이벤트를 사용하여 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-108">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with panelaction events](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - 사용자가 접근성 기능을 토글할 때 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - When a users toggles an accessibility feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - 업데이트된 알림 설정 대화 상자에서 업데이트를 승인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - Acknowledge an update in the we updated a notification setting dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-111">이는 업데이트 알림을 승인하고 전체적인 알림 안정성을 결정하는 데 사용되는 기능 성공 메트릭입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-111">This is a feature success metrics used to acknowledge update notifications and to determine overall notification reliability.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-113">메시지 확장 사용 생성.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-113">Create message extension usage.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-114">작업 메시지 확장 사용.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-114">Action message extension usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - 위치 공유 활성 알림 배너가 해제되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - The location sharing active reminder banner was dismissed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-116">**activityChatClicked** - **활동** 탭에서 비 실시간 채팅을 선택하거나 분할 보기가 표시될 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-116">**activityChatClicked** - Triggered when non-live chat is selected in the **Activity** tab or a split view is shown.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-117">**activityContextMenu** - 활동 피드의 오버플로 작업입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-117">**activityContextMenu** - Overflow actions in the activity feed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-118">**activityFeedClick** - 활동 피드 항목을 탭하고 봇 채팅으로 이동합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-118">**activityFeedClick** - An activity feed item is tapped on and a bot chat is navigated to.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - 피드 항목에서 길게 누르기 제스처를 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - Captures long press gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - 피드 항목에서 살짝 밀기 제스처를 캡쳐합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - Captures swipe gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-121">**activityFilterClick** - 활동 필터 사용법을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-121">**activityFilterClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - 활동 필터 사용량을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - 활동 필터 사용법을 캡처합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - **활동** 탭의 라이브 모임에서 채팅을 선택하면 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - Triggered when chat is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - **활동** 탭의 라이브 모임에서 **세부 사항** 을 선택할 때 트리거됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - Triggered when **Details** is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-126">**activityTabClicked** - 다음 사항 결정에 도움이 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-126">**activityTabClicked** - Helps to determine if:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-127">**활동** 탭이 표시됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-127">The **Activity** tab is shown.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-128">Teams에서 **활동** 탭 이벤트를 캡쳐.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-128">Teams captures an **Activity** tab event.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - **내 활동** 과 **피드** 사이를 전환하기 위해 활동 필터 사용법을 캡쳐합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - Captures activity filter usage to switch between **My Activity** and **Feeds**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-p102">**addChannel** - 채널을 추가합니다. 이 항목은 성공적인 채널 만들기에 대한 성공 데이터를 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-p102">**addChannel** - Adding a channel. This item provides success data around the successful creation of a channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-132">**addMember** - **자세히** 메뉴에서 **사용자 초대** 단추 선택을 트리거합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-132">**addMember** - Triggered the **Invite people** button is selected in the **More** menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-133">**addMembers** - 팀 또는 비공개 채널에 구성원을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-133">**addMembers** - Add members to a team or private channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-134">**addToCalendar** - 개인 일정에 없는 일정 이벤트에 **일정에 추가** 단추를 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-134">**addToCalendar** - Select the **Add to calendar** button for calendar events missing in private calendar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-135">**addToList** - 연락처 목록에 연락처를 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-135">**addToList** - A contact is added to a contact list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-136">**addToMeeting** - 모임 참가자 목록에 **모임에 추가** 단추를 선택합니다(채팅에 참가한 참가자의 경우).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-136">**addToMeeting** - Select the **Add to meeting** button in the participant list for a meeting (for participants who are a part of the chat).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-137">**addUserAsContact** - 연락처의 프로필 카드에 **연락처 추가** 아이콘을 선택하여 연락처를 추가할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-137">**addUserAsContact** - A contact can be added by selecting the **Add contact** icon from the profile card of the contact.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-140">**alertsNavAlert** - 피드 항목을 탭합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-140">**alertsNavAlert** - Tapping on a feed item.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-141">**android: null** - 봇 채팅을 음소거 또는 음소거 해제합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-141">**android: null** - Mute or unmute a bot chat.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-142">이는 채팅에 대한 기존의 원격 분석을 향상시키고 응용 프로그램 정보만을 추가합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-142">This is enhancing existing telemetry around chats only adds application information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - 익명 참가 제공 이름 페이지에서 **모임 참가** 를 선택하거나 이름 대화 상자에서 **확인** 을 탭합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - **Join meeting** is selected on an anonymous join provide name page or **OK** is tapped in the name dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-152">**approveTimeOffRequest** -  FLW(일선 직원) 관리자가 일선 직원의 휴가 요청을 승인할 때 입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-152">**approveTimeOffRequest** -  When a Frontline Worker (FLW) Manager approves a Frontline Worker request to take time off.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-157">**attachmentDeleted** - 작업의 첨부 파일이 성공적으로 삭제되었는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-157">**attachmentDeleted** - Confirms that an attachment in a task was successfully deleted.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-158">**attachmentUpdated** - 작업의 첨부 파일이 성공적으로 업데이트되었는지 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-158">**attachmentUpdated** - Confirms that an attachment in a task was successfully updated.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-160">**audioOnlyPoorNetworkBanner** - 연결 배너가 불량하여 **비디오 끄기** 옵션이 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-160">**audioOnlyPoorNetworkBanner** - The **Video off** option is selected due to a poor connection banner.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - 종료 화면에서 **콜백** 단추를 선택한 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - The number of times the **Callmeback** button was selected at a call end screen.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-164">UFD를 다시 연결하는 데 **전화 접속** 단추가 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-164">The **Dial in** button is selected on the reconnect UFD.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-165">다시 연결되는 동안 **전화 접속** 단추를 선택한 횟수입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-165">The number of times the **Dial In** button was selected while a reconnect is happening.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-166">**autoReconnectDialInonCallDrop** - 통화 연결이 끊긴 UFD에서 **전화 통화** 단추가 선택됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-166">**autoReconnectDialInonCallDrop** - The **Dial in** button is selected on the call disconnected UFD.</span></span>

### <a name="scenario"></a><span data-ttu-id="35c5f-1304">시나리오</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-1304">Scenario</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-1305">PanelAction 이벤트의 속성에 대한 자세한 내용은 [panelaction 시나리오 이벤트를 사용하여 전송된 속성](#properties-sent-with-scenario-events)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-1305">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with scenario events](#properties-sent-with-scenario-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="35c5f-1306">**create_default_plan_and_nav_to_view** - 기본 공유 작업 목록이 성공적으로 만들어졌는지 확인하고 사용자가 작업 후 결과 보기에 도달하는 데 걸린 시간을 확인합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="35c5f-1306">**create_default_plan_and_nav_to_view** - Confirms successful creation of a default shared task list and how long it took for a user to land on the resulting view after action.</span></span>
